D1):** `ChatService.startTurn` writes `messages`, `conversations`, and placeholder `inferences` row SYNCHRONOUSLY in one Prisma `$transaction` BEFORE provider call. Gateway never does this directly.\n2. **`ChatService` is the SOLE writer of `messages.status`** — orchestrator goes through it for terminal state transitions; gateway never touches `messages.status`.\n3. **`StreamOrchestrator` is the SOLE caller of the SDK** — chat service doesn't call SDK directly.\n4. **`message_id` server-assigned, minted BEFORE first provider call** — flows through WS frame envelope, persists as `messages.id` and `inferences.message_id`.\n5. **Cross-user authorization:** every Prisma query in conversations/messages repositories must filter by `userId`. Authorization filter test exists.\n6. **Argon2id for passwords; HMAC-SHA256 for session tokens** (deterministic for lookup; Argon2 won't work for session lookup).\n7. **Opaque session cookie:** httpOnly, SameSite=Lax, secure from env. Cookie name `argus_sid`. Server-side `sessions` table; logout = row delete.\n8. **WS frame envelope** discriminated by `type`: start/token/end/error/cancel-ack outbound, send/cancel inbound. Server-assigned `message_id` + monotonic `seq` per message.\n9. **Cancel UX:** WS cancel frame → orchestrator aborts SDK stream → flush partial content to `messages.content` → emit `canceled` frame → `messages.status='canceled'`.\n10. **Disconnect cleanup:** same flush-then-abort behavior on WS close mid-stream.\n\n## Builder-flagged concerns (verify in your review)\n\n1. **`MessageDto` hydration gap** — `errorCode`/`provider`/`model` come from `inferences` table but `MessagesRepository` only reads `messages`. **Currently being fixed in a parallel agent dispatch — verify the fix landed if the diff includes a new commit beyond `653aa20`.**\n2. **In-memory Prisma fixture** in `apps/api/test/fixtures/prisma-test-client.ts` — won't catch real Postgres semantics.\n3. **WS gateway uses raw `client.on('message')`** instead of `@SubscribeMessage` — bypasses Nest interceptors.\n4. **Outbox guarantee under crash** — placeholder `inferences` row stuck at `status='streaming'` if api dies between tx commit and SDK call.\n5. **No rate limiting on `/auth/*`** — Argon2 burst = DoS vector.\n6. **Cross-port cookie behavior** — same host (`localhost`) is fine; cross-host (`api.example.com` + `example.com`) needs `SameSite=None` + `Secure`.\n\n## Output format (terse, no preamble)\n\n### 1. codex designs the actual tests via the wrapper\n34\t\n35\t## File Structure\n36\t\n37\t```\n38\tapps/api/\n39\t  src/\n40\t    main.ts                                    # Nest bootstrap; runs seed before listen\n41\t    app.module.ts                              # root module: Auth, Conversations, Chat\n42\t    bootstrap/\n43\t      seed.ts                                  # idempotent demo-user seed\n44\t    common/\n45\t      prisma.service.ts                        # PrismaClient lifecycle (from packages/db)\n46\t      session-cookie.ts                        # cookie name + serialization constants\n47\t      authorization.filter.ts                  # user-scoped query helper / repo factory\n48\t    auth/\n49\t      auth.module.ts\n50\t      auth.controller.ts                       # POST /auth/signup, /auth/login, /auth/logout\n51\t      auth.service.ts                          # hash, verify, issueSession, revokeSession\n52\t      password.ts                              # Argon2id wrapper (hash, verify)\n53\t      session.repository.ts                    # Prisma access for sessions table\n54\t      session.guard.ts                         # REST guard: cookie → user_id on req\n55\t      ws-session.ts                            # WS handshake cookie → user_id resolver\n56\t      dto/\n57\t        signup.dto.ts                          # zod schema for signup body\n58\t        login.dto.ts                           # zod schema for login body\n59\t    conversations/\n60\t      conversations.module.ts\n61\t      conversations.controller.ts              # REST CRUD; SessionGuard applied\n62\t      conversations.repository.ts              # user-scoped Prisma access\n63\t      dto/\n64\t        create-conversation.dto.ts\n65\t        update-conversation.dto.ts\n66\t    chat/\n67\t      chat.module.ts\n68\t      chat.gateway.ts                          # @WebSocketGateway; cookie auth on handshake\n69\t      chat.service.ts                          # owns message_id mint + messages.status writes\n70\t      frame-builder.ts                         # pure helpers: build start/token/end/error/cancel-ack frames\n71\t      seq-counter.ts                           # per-message monotonic seq source\n72\t      stream-orchestrator.ts                   # wraps SDK stream, handles cancel + disconnect flush\n73\t  test/\n74\t    auth/\n75\t      password.test.ts\n76\t      auth.service.test.ts\n77\t      session.guard.test.ts\n78\t      ws-session.test.ts\n79\t    bootstrap/\n80\t      seed.test.ts\n81\t    conversations/\n82\t      conversations.repository.test.ts\n83\t    chat/\n84\t      frame-builder.test.ts\n85\t      seq-counter.test.ts\n86\t      chat.service.test.ts\n87\t      stream-orchestrator.test.ts\n88\t    common/\n89\t      authorization.filter.test.ts             # table-driven cross-user rejection\n90\t    fixtures/\n91\t      prisma-test-client.ts                    # spins ephemeral DB or uses in-memory mock\n92\t```\n93\t\n94\t## Dependencies\n95\t\n96\t- `packages/db` — `PrismaClient` and generated types for `users`, `sessions`, `conversations`, `messages`, `inferences`. The schema lives in the backend-infra LLD; this LLD assumes the client is exported.\n97\t- `packages/sdk` — exports `chat.stream({ messages, conversationId, turnIndex, userId, signal }) → AsyncIterable<{ token } | { done, providerMeta }>` (or equivalent). This LLD consumes that surface and treats the iterator as the only contact point with provider logic.\n98\t- `packages/contracts` — exports zod schemas + TS types for inbound and outbound WS frames (`start`, `token`, `end`, `error`, `cancel`, `cancel-ack`). This LLD imports the types; it does not define them.\n99\t\n100\t---\n101\t\n102\t## Tasks\n103\t\n104\t### Task 1 (RED): Failing test for Argon2id password hash uniqueness\n105\t**Files:** `apps/api/test/auth/password.test.ts`\n106\t**What to do:** Write a failing test asserting `hashPassword(plain)` produces an Argon2id-formatted string starting with `$argon2id$` and that two calls on the same plaintext yield different outputs (salt randomness).\n107\t**Acceptance:** Test exists, runs, fails because `apps/api/src/auth/password.ts` does not yet exist or `hashPassword` is unimplemented.\n108\t**Verify:** `pnpm --filter @argus/api test password.test` reports the expected failure.\n109\t\n110\t### Task 2 (GREEN): Implement Argon2id `hashPassword`\n111\t**Files:** `apps/api/src/auth/password.ts`\n112\t**What to do:** Implement `hashPassword(plain: string): Promise<string>` using `argon2` library in `argon2id` mode with library-recommended memory/time/parallelism defaults.\n113\t**Acceptance:** Task 1's test passes; no other tests broken.\n114\t**Verify:** `pnpm --filter @argus/api test` and `pnpm --filter @argus/api type-check`.\n115\t\n116\t### Task 3 (RED): Failing test for password verify (correct + incorrect)\n117\t**Files:** `apps/api/test/auth/password.test.ts`\n118\t**What to do:** Add failing assertions that `verifyPassword(hash, plain)` returns `true` for the matching plaintext and `false` for a mismatched one.\n119\t**Acceptance:** Test exists, runs, fails because `verifyPassword` is unimplemented.\n120\t**Verify:** `pnpm --filter @argus/api test password.test` reports the expected failure on the new assertions.\n121\t\n122\t### Task 4 (GREEN): Implement `verifyPassword`\n123\t**Files:** `apps/api/src/auth/password.ts`\n124\t**What to do:** Add `verifyPassword(hash: string, plain: string): Promise<boolean>` that delegates to `argon2.verify` and returns its boolean result, catching verify errors as `false`.\n125\t**Acceptance:** Task 3 passes; On miss, close with 4401 policy violation.\n11\t//   - On hit, stash userId + per-connection orchestrator registry on the\n12\t//     socket.\n13\t//\n14\t// Frame handling:\n15\t//   - Parse JSON, validate via WsFrameInboundSchema.\n16\t//   - 'send'   → ownership check on conversationId, call chat.startTurn,\n17\t//                start StreamOrchestrator.\n18\t//   - 'cancel' → look up orchestrator by messageId, call .cancel().\n19\t//   - Anything else → ignore (the schema's discriminated union rejects\n20\t//                       unknown types at parse time).\n21\t//\n22\t// Disconnect:\n23\t//   - handleDisconnect: call .onDisconnect() on every active orchestrator\n24\t//     for that connection. Release per-message seq counters.\n25\timport {\n26\t  Logger,\n27\t  type OnModuleInit,\n28\t} from '@nestjs/common';\n29\timport {\n30\t  OnGatewayConnection,\n31\t  OnGatewayDisconnect,\n32\t  WebSocketGateway,\n33\t} from '@nestjs/websockets';\n34\timport type { IncomingMessage } from 'http';\n35\timport type { WebSocket, RawData } from 'ws';\n36\timport { ChatService } from './chat.service';\n37\timport { SeqCounterRegistry } from './seq-counter';\n38\timport { StreamOrchestrator } from './stream-orchestrator';\n39\timport { resolveWsUser } from '../auth/ws-session';\n40\timport { AuthService } from '../auth/auth.service';\n41\timport { ConversationsRepository } from '../conversations/conversations.repository';\n42\timport { WS_PATH, WsFrameInboundSchema, type WsFrameOutbound } from '@argus/contracts';\n43\timport { chat as sdkChat } from '@argus/sdk';\n44\timport { captureApiError, withWsScope } from '../observability/sentry';\n45\timport { buildErrorFrame } from './frame-builder';\n46\t\n47\tinterface ChatClient extends WebSocket {\n48\t  data?: ChatClientData;\n49\t}\n50\t\n51\tinterface ChatClientData {\n52\t  userId: string;\n53\t  orchestrators: Map<string, StreamOrchestrator>;\n54\t}\n55\t\n56\tconst WS_POLICY_VIOLATION = 1008;\n57\tconst WS_INTERNAL_ERROR = 1011;\n58\t\n59\t@WebSocketGateway({ path: WS_PATH })\n60\texport class ChatGateway implements OnGatewayConnection, OnGatewayDisconnect, OnModuleInit {\n61\t  private readonly logger = new Logger(ChatGateway.name);\n62\t\n63\t  constructor(\n64\t    private readonly chatService: ChatService,\n65\t    private readonly seqRegistry: SeqCounterRegistry,\n66\t    private readonly auth: AuthService,\n67\t    private readonly conversations: ConversationsRepository,\n68\t  ) {}\n69\t\n70\t  onModuleInit(): void {\n71\t    this.logger.log(`ChatGateway ready — WS path=${WS_PATH}`);\n72\t  }\n73\t\n74\t  async handleConnection(client: ChatClient, req: IncomingMessage): Promise<void> {\n75\t    try {\n76\t      const userId = await resolveWsUser(req.headers, this.auth);\n77\t      if (!userId) {\n78\t        client.close(WS_POLICY_VIOLATION, 'unauthenticated');\n79\t        return;\n80\t      }\n81\t      client.data = { userId, orchestrators: new Map() };\n82\t      // Bind our own raw message handler. We bypass @SubscribeMessage because\n83\t      // @nestjs/platform-ws's default dispatcher expects { event, data } and\n84\t      // our wire contract uses a `type` discriminator (see @argus/contracts).\n85\t      client.on('message', (raw: RawData) => {\n86\t        void this.onClientMessage(client, raw);\n87\t      });\n88\t    } catch (err) {\n89\t      captureApiError({\n90\t        err,\n91\t        feature: 'chat',\n92\t        layer: 'gateway',\n93\t        extra: { stage: 'handleConnection' },\n94\t      });\n95\t      try {\n96\t        client.close(WS_INTERNAL_ERROR, 'connect failure');\n97\t      } catch {\n98\t        // ignore — socket may already be closed\n99\t      }\n100\t    }\n101\t  }\n102\t\n103\t  private async onClientMessage(client: ChatClient, raw: RawData): Promise<void> {\n104\t    const data = client.data;\n105\t    if (!data) {\n106\t      client.close(WS_POLICY_VIOLATION, 'unauthenticated');\n107\t      return;\n108\t    }\n109\t    let payload: unknown;\n110\t    try {\n111\t      payload = JSON.parse(raw.toString());\n112\t    } catch (err) {\n113\t      captureApiError({\n114\t        err,\n115\t        feature: 'chat',\n116\t        layer: 'gateway',\n117\t        extra: { stage: 'json-parse' },\n118\t      });\n119\t      return;\n120\t    }\n121\t    const parsed = WsFrameInboundSchema.safeParse(payload);\n122\t    if (!parsed.success) {\n123\t      captureApiError({\n124\t        err: new Error('invalid_frame'),\n125\t        feature: 'chat',\n126\t        layer: 'gateway',\n127\t        extra: { stage: 'schema-parse', issues: parsed.error.issues.map((i) => i.message).join(';') },\n128\t      });\n129\t      return;\n130\t    }\n131\t    const frame = parsed.data;\n132\t    await withWsScope(\n133\t      {\n134\t        feature: 'chat',\n135\t        event: 'frame',\n136\t        userId: data.userId,\n137\t        frameType: frame.type,\n138\t      },\n139\t      async () => {\n140\t        if (frame.type === 'send') {\n141\t          await this.handleSend(client, data, frame);\n142\t        } else if (frame.type === 'cancel') {\n143\t          await this.handleCancel(data, frame.messageId);\n144\t        }\n145\t      },\n146\t    );\n147\t  }\n148\t\n149\t  async handleDisconnect(client: ChatClient): Promise<void> {\n150\t    const data = client.data;\n151\t    if (!data) return;\n152\t    await withWsScope(\n153\t      { feature: 'chat', event: 'disconnect', userId: data.userId },\n154\t      async () => {\n155\t        for (const [messageId, orch] of data.orchestrators) {\n156\t          try {\n157\t            await orch.onDisconnect();\n158\t          } catch (err) {\n159\t            captureApiError({\n160\t              err,\n161\t              feature: 'chat',\n162\t              layer: 'gateway',\n163\t              extra: { stage: 'onDisconnect', messageId },\n164\t            });\n165\t          }\n166\t Placeholder inferences row — outbox-pattern. Projection consumer\n88\t      //    enriches via OTel span (message.id attribute join).\n89\t      await tx.inference.create({\n90\t        data: {\n91\t          messageId: assistantMessageId,\n92\t          conversationId: input.conversationId,\n93\t          userId: input.userId,\n94\t          provider: 'pending',\n95\t          model: 'pending',\n96\t          status: 'streaming',\n97\t          startedAt: now,\n98\t        },\n99\t      });\n100\t    });\n101\t\n102\t    return { userMessageId, assistantMessageId };\n103\t  }\n104\t\n105\t  async completeTurn(messageId: string, content: string): Promise<void> {\n106\t    await this.prisma.db.message.update({\n107\t      where: { id: messageId },\n108\t      data: {\n109\t        content,\n110\t        status: 'complete',\n111\t        completedAt: new Date(),\n112\t      },\n113\t    });\n114\t  }\n115\t\n116\t  async cancelTurn(messageId: string, partialContent: string): Promise<void> {\n117\t    await this.prisma.db.message.update({\n118\t      where: { id: messageId },\n119\t      data: {\n120\t        content: partialContent,\n121\t        status: 'canceled',\n122\t        completedAt: new Date(),\n123\t      },\n124\t    });\n125\t  }\n126\t\n127\t  /**\n128\t   * Mark a streaming message as failed and flush any partial content.\n129\t   *\n130\t   * `errorCode` is accepted for API completeness (the WS error frame carries\n131\t   * it). The orchestrator owns a single AbortController per\n15\t// invocation; sdkStream.signal is the same controller's signal.\n16\timport type { ChatStreamChunk, ProviderMeta } from '@argus/sdk';\n17\timport { ChatService } from './chat.service';\n18\timport { SeqCounterRegistry } from './seq-counter';\n19\timport {\n20\t  buildCancelAckFrame,\n21\t  buildEndFrame,\n22\t  buildErrorFrame,\n23\t  buildStartFrame,\n24\t  buildTokenFrame,\n25\t} from './frame-builder';\n26\timport type { WsFrameOutbound } from '@argus/contracts';\n27\timport { captureApiError } from '../observability/sentry';\n28\t\n29\t/** What the orchestrator emits — gateway forwards over WS, tests assert on it. */\n30\texport type Emit = (frame: WsFrameOutbound) => void;\n31\t\n32\texport interface RunStreamInput {\n33\t  messageId: string;\n34\t  conversationId: string;\n35\t  provider: string;\n36\t  model: string;\n37\t  sdkStream: AsyncIterable<ChatStreamChunk>;\n38\t  /** Surface the underlying AbortController so we can stop the SDK iterator. */\n39\t  abort: AbortController;\n40\t  emit: Emit;\n41\t}\n42\t\n43\ttype Terminal = 'complete' | 'canceled' | 'failed' | 'disconnected';\n44\t\n45\texport class StreamOrchestrator {\n46\t  private terminal: Terminal | null = null;\n47\t  private partialContent = '';\n48\t\n49\t  constructor(\n50\t    private readonly chat: ChatService,\n51\t    private readonly seqRegistry: SeqCounterRegistry,\n52\t    private readonly input: RunStreamInput,\n53\t  ) {}\n54\t\n55\t  /**\n56\t   * Drive the SDK iterator to completion. Resolves when the terminal frame\n57\t   * has been emitted (or when disconnect has been observed — in which case\n58\t   * no end frame is emitted).\n59\t   */\n60\t  async runStream(): Promise<void> {\n61\t    const counter = this.seqRegistry.for(this.input.messageId);\n62\t\n63\t    // Start frame — seq 0.\n64\t    counter.next(); // consume 0\n65\t    this.emit(\n66\t      buildStartFrame({\n67\t        messageId: this.input.messageId,\n68\t        conversationId: this.input.conversationId,\n69\t        provider: this.input.provider,\n70\t        model: this.input.model,\n71\t      }),\n72\t    );\n73\t\n74\t    let providerMeta: ProviderMeta | null = null;\n75\t\n76\t    try {\n77\t      for await (const chunk of this.input.sdkStream) {\n78\t        // Race guard: if we've already entered a terminal state (cancel /\n79\t        // disconnect arrived between iterator yields), drop the chunk.\n80\t        if (this.terminal !== null) return;\n81\t        if (chunk.type === 'token') {\n82\t          this.partialContent += chunk.content;\n83\t          this.emit(buildTokenFrame(this.input.messageId, counter.next(), chunk.content));\n84\t        } else if (chunk.type === 'done') {\n85\t          providerMeta = chunk.providerMeta;\n86\t        }\n87\t      }\n88\t    } catch (err) {\n89\t      // SDK threw — could be pre-first-token or mid-stream. Either way,\n90\t      // flush partial + emit error + end.\n91\t      if (this.terminal !== null) return; // disconnect already handled\n92\t      const code = errorCodeOf(err);\n93\t      this.terminal = 'failed';\n94\t      try {\n95\t        await this.chat.failTurn(this.input.messageId, this.partialContent, code);\n96\t      } catch (dbErr) {\n97\t        captureApiError({\n98\t          err: dbErr,\n99\t          feature: 'chat',\n100\t          layer: 'orchestrator',\n101\t          extra: { stage: 'failTurn-after-sdk-error', messageId: this.input.messageId },\n102\t        });\n103\t      }\n104\t      captureApiError({\n105\t        err,\n106\t        feature: 'chat',\n107\t        layer: 'orchestrator',\n108\t        extra: { stage: 'sdk-stream', messageId: this.input.messageId, errorCode: code },\n109\t      });\n110\t      this.emit(buildErrorFrame(this.input.messageId, code, errorMessageOf(err)));\n111\t      this.emit(buildEndFrame(this.input.messageId, counter.next(), 'failed'));\n112\t      this.seqRegistry.release(this.input.messageId);\n113\t      return;\n114\t    }\n115\t\n116\t    if (this.terminal !== null) return; // cancel/disconnect raced with last token\n117\t    this.terminal = 'complete';\n118\t    try {\n119\t      await this.chat.completeTurn(this.input.messageId, this.partialContent);\n120\t    } catch (err) {\n121\t      captureApiError({\n122\t        err,\n123\t        feature: 'chat',\n124\t        layer: 'orchestrator',\n125\t        extra: {\n126\t          stage: 'completeTurn',\n127\t          messageId: this.input.messageId,\n128\t          providerMeta: providerMeta ? JSON.stringify(providerMeta) : undefined,\n129\t        },\n130\t      });\n131\t    }\n132\t    this.emit(buildEndFrame(this.input.messageId, counter.next(), 'complete'));\n133\t    this.seqRegistry.release(this.input.messageId);\n134\t  }\n135\t\n136\t  /**\n137\t   * Cancel an in-flight stream. Idempotent — repeated calls after terminal\n138\t   * resolve to no-op.\n139\t   */\n140\t  async cancel(): Promise<void> {\n141\t    if (this.terminal !== null) return;\n142\t    this.terminal = 'canceled';\n143\t    this.input.abort.abort();\n144\t    try {\n145\t      await this.chat.cancelTurn(this.input.messageId, this.partialContent);\n146\t    } catch (err) {\n147\t      captureApiError({\n148\t        err,\n149\t        feature: 'chat',\n150\t        layer: 'orchestrator',\n151\t        extra: { stage: 'cancelTurn', messageId: this.input.messageId },\n152\t      });\n153\t    }\n154\t    const counter = this.seqRegistry.for(this.input.messageId);\n155\t    this.emit(buildCancelAckFrame(this.input.messageId));\n156\t    this.emit(buildEndFrame(this.input.messageId, counter.next(), 'canceled'));\n157\t    this.seqRegistry.release(this.input.messageId);\n158\t  }\n159\t\n160\t  /**\n161\t   * Client disconnected mid-stream. We must persist whatever we have and\n162\t   * stop the SDK iterator; we MUST NOT emit further frames (socket is\n163\t   * gone — any emit could throw on a half-closed socket).\n164\t   */\n165\t  async onDisconnect(): Promise<void> {\n166\t    if (this.terminal !== null) return;\n167\t    this.terminal = 'disconnected';\n168\t    this.input.abort.abort();\n169\t    try {\n170\t      await this.chat.failTurn(this.input.messageId, this.partialContent, 'client_disconnected');\n171\t    } catch (err) {\n172\t      captureApiError({\n173\t        err,\n174\t        feature: 'chat',\n175\t        layer: 'orchestrator',\n176\t        extra: { stage: 'failTurn-disconnect', messageId: this.input.messageId },\n177\t      });\n178\t    }\n179\t    this.seqRegistry.release(this.input.messageId);\n180\t  }\n181\t\n182\t  isTerminal(): boolean {\n183\t    return this.terminal !== null;\n184\t  }\n185\t\n186\t  private emit(frame: WsFrameOutbound): void {\n187\t    if (this.terminal === 'disconnected') return; // never emit after disconnect\n188\t    try {\n189\t      this.input.emit(frame);\n190\t    } catch (err) {\n191\t      // The socket may have closed between emits — capture but don't crash\n192\t      // the orchestrator. The next emit will hit the same guard.\n193\t      captureApiError({\n194\t        err,\n195\t        feature: 'chat',\n196\t        layer: 'orchestrator',\n197\t        extra: { stage: 'emit', messageId: this.input.messageId, frameType: frame.type },\n198\t      });\n199\t    }\n200\t  }\n201\t}\n202\t\n203\tfunction errorCodeOf(err: unknown): string {\n204\t  if (typeof err === 'object' && err !== null) {\n205\t    const code = (err as { code?: unknown }).code;\n206\t    if (typeof code === 'string') return code;\n207\t  }\n208\t  return 'sdk_error';\n209\t}\n210\t\n211\tfunction errorMessageOf(err: unknown): string | undefined {\n212\t  if (err instanceof Error) return err.message;\n213\t  return undefined;\n214\t}\n215\t"}]},"uuid":"273dd3d0-523f-46df-97ea-2f656cbabc69","timestamp":"2026-05-23T19:42:57.600Z","sourceToolAssistantUUID":"4460870f-471f-4c53-be63-e31cbb239bef","userType":"external","entrypoint":"cli","cwd":"/Users/lego/Desktop/personal-projects/argus/.worktrees/phase-a-build","sessionId":"11d45e97-2fff-4114-aafb-b68d865b0473","version":"2.1.150","gitBranch":"HEAD"}

{"parentUuid":"6d06ebb3-002f-4e23-ba7e-d5aff2189170","isSidechain":true,"agentId":"a67efae93e47d4e8b","message":{"model":"claude-opus-4-7","id":"msg_01LDxU6kx2JaZgGK77Kxfbws","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"text","text":"I now have everything I need. Let me write the review.\n\n---\n\n### 1. LLD adherence violations\n\n- **Task 28 controller drops `errorCode`/`provider`/`model`** — `MessagesRepository.listForConversation` was patched to hydrate these from `inferences` (`messages.repository.ts:54-85`), but `conversations.controller.ts:46-56` `toMessageDto` never copies them onto the wire DTO. The patch is wasted; frontend-web Task 43 (\"provider/model label\") + Task 45 (\"interrupted marker keyed off `errorCode === 'client_disconnected'`\") still get `undefined`.\n- **Task 28 `getById` hydration is hardcoded null** — `messages.repository.ts:87-98` returns `errorCode/provider/model: null` literally, never querying `inferences`. So even if a future controller path uses `getById` it can't satisfy the contract.\n- **Task 28 `MessageListResponse.omittedCount` never populated** — contract advertises it (`conversations.ts:71-76`), the LLD references it as the source for the \"N earlier messages omitted from context\" indicator (frontend-web Task 42), but the controller does not compute or return it. Frontend will silently get `undefined` forever.\n- **Task 55 acceptance criterion \"start frame within 500ms of sending a `send` payload\"** — start frame contains `provider: 'mock'`, `model: 'mock-1'` hardcoded in `chat.gateway.ts:231-232` BEFORE the SDK has yielded anything. The real SDK is supposed to surface provider/model on `done`. Per LLD this is acceptable for Phase A, but it should be wired through `providerMeta` once available — currently `providerMeta` in `stream-orchestrator.ts:74-86` is captured then discarded (only used in a Sentry `extra`).\n- **Builder-flagged concern #3 confirmed (raw `client.on('message')`)** — `chat.gateway.ts:85` bypasses `@SubscribeMessage`, so any future Nest interceptors/guards/pipes will not run on inbound frames. The LLD itself accepts this trade-off but it should be documented as a hard architectural boundary (e.g., a comment + a `@nestjs/websockets` guard list in `chat.module.ts`).\n\n### 2. Correctness bugs\n\n1. **`MessageDto` hydration gap PERSISTS** — see LLD violation #1 above. The \"parallel agent dispatch\" did patch the repository but never updated the controller mapper. **`conversations.controller.ts:46-56`** must add `errorCode: row.errorCode, provider: row.provider, model: row.model` to `toMessageDto`. This is the only thing standing between the schema contract and the frontend.\n2. **Late tokens after `cancel()` race the SDK's own micro-yields** — `stream-orchestrator.ts:140-158` sets `this.terminal = 'canceled'`, calls `abort.abort()`, then `await this.chat.cancelTurn(...)`. Between the abort and the `cancelTurn` await, the active `for await` loop in `runStream` may pull one more chunk (since `aborted` is only checked inside the loop after each yield, not synchronously). The `partialContent` recorded by `cancelTurn` (`this.partialContent`) is then *stale* — it may not include the token that arrived during the await. The cancel-ack/end frames are also fine because `terminal !== null` blocks emit-late, but `messages.content` may miss the last visible token the user saw. Note: the test passes because the mock stream pauses on a gate, but a real SDK that yields tightly will hit this.\n3. **`cancel()` reads `this.partialContent` once, before await** — same root as #2: capture `const partial = this.partialContent` immediately after `abort`, then run `cancelTurn(messageId, partial)`. The current code passes `this.partialContent` to `cancelTurn` synchronously which actually does close the race for the call argument — but the underlying invariant (\"DB content == what the user saw\") only holds if the user's WS stream is in lockstep with `runStream`'s state. Since `runStream` may still process one chunk and *emit a token frame* after `cancel()` is called but before `terminal` is checked at the top of the next iteration, the user could see N+1 tokens while the DB stores N. Fix: check `this.terminal` immediately after `await this.input.sdkStream` yields, AND inside the `if (chunk.type === 'token')` branch before mutating `partialContent`.\n4. **`buildSessionCookie` `maxAge` and `sessions.expiresAt` use the same epoch reset** — `session-cookie.ts:23` writes `maxAge: SESSION_TTL_MS/1000` on every Set-Cookie, but the DB row's `expiresAt` was set at session creation time. A session created 29 days ago and used today will re-issue a cookie with 30 more days, but the DB row still expires tomorrow. The `findUserIdByToken` check at `session.repository.ts:61` will reject one day later. Either (a) refresh `expiresAt` on every `findUserIdByToken` hit, or (b) drop the `maxAge` re-issue and let the cookie expire when the DB row does. Currently the user gets silently kicked out before the cookie says they should be.\n5. **`startTurn` does NOT verify `conversation.userId` matches** — `chat.service.ts:48-100` accepts `userId` and `conversationId` as inputs and trusts both. The gateway *does* check ownership via `conversations.getByIdForUser` (`chat.gateway.ts:187`), but `ChatService.startTurn` is now a footgun — if any future caller (HTTP-triggered chat? job runner? test) passes a mismatched pair, the transaction will create a `messages` row with `userId=A` inside a `conversations` row owned by `userId=B`. The `updateMany` on `conversation` filters by `{ id, userId }` so the conversation update silently fails (count=0) and the messages get orphaned. Add a defensive `getByIdForUser` inside `startTurn` and throw if it returns null — or document the precondition with a runtime assert.\n6. **Outbox crash window is wider than builder flagged** — between the `$transaction` commit (`chat.service.ts:53-100`) and the SDK call (`chat.gateway.ts:219`), an api crash leaves an `inferences` row with `status='streaming'`, `provider='pending'`, `model='pending'` forever, plus a `messages` row with `status='streaming'`. There is NO reaper, NO timeout, NO retry — the projection consumer (workers) only enriches rows when an OTel span arrives, and a span never will if the SDK never ran. Phase B should add a reaper; for Phase A document this as a known data-quality hazard and add a sentinel for the consumer to skip \"pending\" rows.\n7. **WS gateway returns an error frame with a sentinel `'00000000-...0000'` `messageId`** — `chat.gateway.ts:191, 213`. The frame validates against the schema (it's a valid UUID), but no client could ever bind it to a logical request. Either (a) frame errors before `message_id` mint should not require `messageId` (schema change), or (b) the gateway should mint the messageId *before* the conversation-existence check and pass it through so all error frames are correlatable. Today the web client sees an `error` frame with messageId `0000…` and has no way to associate it with the `send` that triggered it.\n8. **No outbound `end` frame on the error paths in the gateway** — `chat.gateway.ts:189-194` and `211-214` emit only `error` frames. Per the LLD task 53/54, every terminal must be an `error` frame followed by an `end` frame (status='failed'). The stream-orchestrator does this correctly (`stream-orchestrator.ts:110-111`); the gateway pre-orchestrator paths do not. Frontend-web has no way to know the stream is finished.\n9. **`computeTurnIndex` is a `_` stub returning `0`** — `chat.gateway.ts:269-273`. Every turn the SDK sees `turnIndex=0`. The mock SDK ignores it, but the real SDK (per `packages/sdk/src/index.ts:39`) treats it as load-bearing for context windowing. Phase B will fall over silently if no one notices this.\n10. **`session.findFirst({ where: { tokenHash } })` is not unique-constrained at the query level** — `session.repository.ts:55-57` uses `findFirst` not `findUnique` even though `schema.prisma` shows `Session.tokenHash` is `@unique`. Cosmetic but `findUnique` is more efficient and signals intent.\n11. **`InMemoryPrisma.user.create` does not generate `id` via `randomUUID()` when `args.data.id` is absent** — actually it does (`prisma-test-client.ts:127`). But the `signup` flow in real code lets Prisma generate the UUID via `@default(uuid())`. Tests will pass on in-memory and may fail on real Postgres if a test ever passes `data: { id: ... }` explicitly. Edge-case, not blocking.\n12. **`PrismaService` is registered separately in 4 modules** — `app.module.ts:14`, `auth.module.ts:13`, `conversations.module.ts:11`, `chat.module.ts:11`. Each module gets its own `PrismaService` instance. The underlying `prisma` client is module-global so the connection pool is shared (good), but `onModuleDestroy` will be called 4 times → `$disconnect` 4 times. With `@Optional() @Inject(PRISMA_CLIENT_TOKEN)` in the constructor that's harmless, but it's noisy and indicates a missing `@Global()` decorator on a single `CommonModule` providing `PrismaService`.\n13. **`errorMessageOf` returns `undefined`** — `stream-orchestrator.ts:211-214`, then `buildErrorFrame(..., undefined)` constructs `{ type:'error', messageId, errorCode }`. The schema accepts the absent message (it's optional), so OK; but `frame-builder.ts:54-65` uses `...(message !== undefined ? { message } : {})` which is correct. No bug, just verifying.\n14. **`isUniqueViolation` only checks `code === 'P2002'`** — `auth.service.ts:33-35`. Does not verify `meta.target` includes `email`. If a future unique constraint (say, on a denormalized column) hits the same code, the user will see \"email taken\" for an unrelated collision. Add `meta?.target?.includes('email')` check.\n15. **`signup` returns 201 with cookie even if `sessions.create` raced into a P2002 on `tokenHash`** — extremely improbable (32 random bytes), but the `signup` code path does not handle a sessions.create error specifically; it would 500. Cosmetic.\n16. **In-memory `clone()` deep-roundtrips through JSON** — `prisma-test-client.ts:87-91` serializes dates via ISO then parses back. The regex `/^\\d{4}-\\d{2}-\\d{2}T/` will also re-`new Date()` ANY string starting with that pattern (e.g., a user-supplied `email` like `2026-05-23T@example.com`). Vanishingly small risk but a real bug if you ever store a free-text field starting with a date.\n\n### 3. Cross-LLD coordination risk\n\n- **`@argus/sdk` `chat.stream` surface is fixed by the stub** — `packages/sdk/src/index.ts:35-44` defines `ChatStreamRequest` with `messageId` as **required**. The orchestrator passes `messageId` (good). The full SDK LLD MUST honor this — if it drops/renames the field, the apps/api gateway breaks. Recommend snapshotting this interface in the SDK LLD's \"Inputs\" section.\n- **WS `start` frame contract says `provider`/`model` are free-text** — the gateway hardcodes `'mock'/'mock-1'` and never overwrites with the SDK's `providerMeta`. Frontend-web Task 43 keys the per-message provider/model label off this; for Phase A it'll always say \"mock\". OK for stub, but flag the swap-in point.\n- **`ChatStreamChunk` `{type:'done'}` providerMeta has `promptTokens`/`completionTokens` as optional** — the orchestrator never propagates them. The projection consumer is supposed to fill `inferences.{prompt_tokens,completion_tokens}` from the OTel span. Phase A's stub SDK doesn't emit spans, so these columns stay null forever in dev. Document as expected.\n- **`WS_PATH` constant is shared** — good; `chat.gateway.ts:59` imports from `@argus/contracts`. Web client and api can't drift.\n- **`messages.error_code` column does NOT exist in the schema** — confirmed by reading `packages/db/schema.prisma` excerpt. The LLD's Open Question said \"if the column does not exist, Task 45/46 drop the column reference.\" `chat.service.ts:135-144` correctly accepts `_errorCode` and doesn't write it. But this means a `client_disconnected` is reconstructible ONLY by joining through `inferences.error_code` (which is NOT written by `failTurn` either — the orchestrator only updates messages). Result: history hydration on a disconnected message will return `errorCode: null` from the inferences-side projection because no one ever wrote it. The frontend's \"Retry\" button (frontend-web Task 45) keyed on `errorCode === 'client_disconnected'` will never light up. **This is a real cross-LLD break.** Either (a) `failTurn` must also `update inference.errorCode`, or (b) the LLD must add a column to `messages`.\n- **`omittedCount` field is declared in the contract** but no API path computes it — frontend will see `undefined` and silently render no \"N earlier messages omitted\" banner.\n- **PORT** — `main.ts:69` defaults to 4000. Web client/dev compose must match. Not flagged in any contract — recommend constant in contracts.\n\n### 4. Security\n\n- **`SESSION_SECRET` env-var is required but not validated at boot** — `session.repository.ts:36-41` throws on `hashToken` invocation if `SESSION_SECRET` is unset. Boot succeeds, the DB ping succeeds, the seed succeeds (it doesn't hash tokens), the API listens, the **first login request** crashes. Fix: validate `SESSION_SECRET` in `main.ts` alongside the DB ping.\n- **No rate limiting on `/auth/*`** (builder-flagged) — confirmed. `auth.controller.ts` has no `@Throttle`, no middleware, no IP-based gating. Argon2id is ~50ms/op; an attacker burst of 20 requests/sec pegs a CPU core. Phase A acceptable only if dev-only; for any internet exposure must add `@nestjs/throttler` on `signup`/`login` (3-5 req/min/IP).\n- **No CSRF protection on POST `/auth/login` or `/auth/logout`** — cookie is `SameSite=Lax`, which prevents cross-site auto-submit of POST forms, **but** a malicious site can trigger logout via a top-level navigation (POST→`<form action=\"/auth/logout\">` is blocked by Lax for cross-site, OK). Login from a malicious site would not transmit the existing cookie due to Lax. Probably fine for Phase A; double-check when `SameSite=None` becomes necessary (cross-host deploy — builder-flagged #6).\n- **`/auth/login` returns the same `InvalidCredentialsError` for unknown email + wrong password** — good, enumeration-resistant. Dummy hash verify equalizes timing — good.\n- **`/auth/signup` always returns 409 on duplicate email** — this IS user enumeration. An attacker can probe whether `alice@example.com` exists by attempting signup. Mitigations: (a) return 201 with a no-op cookie and send \"if this is a new account, check your email\" workflow (requires email infra), or (b) accept as a documented trade-off (most apps do). Flag, don't block.\n- **`session.deleteByToken` does not filter by `userId`** — `session.repository.ts:65-68` deletes any session matching the hash. Since `tokenHash` includes the HMAC secret, an attacker can't forge a match without the secret. OK as-is.\n- **`SessionGuard` reads `req.cookies` populated by `cookie-parser`** — middleware order is `app.use(cookieParser())` then routes, so this works. WS handshake uses `extractSessionCookie` directly on raw headers — also good.\n- **`SESSION_SECRET` rotation will instantaneously invalidate every active session** — no key rotation strategy. Out of scope for Phase A but document.\n- **Cookie is httpOnly + `SameSite=Lax` + `Secure` only when `NODE_ENV=production`** — correct. Cross-port (`localhost:3000`↔`localhost:4000`) works because same host. Cross-host requires `SameSite=None` + `Secure` — builder-flagged correctly.\n- **Logout always sets cleared cookie even on unknown token** — `auth.controller.ts:87-98` correctly idempotent. Returns 204.\n- **`ConversationsController.rename` returns 404 on cross-user attempts** — `conversations.controller.ts:101-114` — good, no existence-leak.\n- **`captureApiError` strips request body on Sentry capture** — good, prevents plaintext password leak (observed in `observability/sentry.ts`).\n- **No request-body size limit beyond zod `max(64_000)` on WS `send.content`** — REST endpoints fall back to Express default (100kb-ish). Sufficient for Phase A but document.\n- **`SignupRequestSchema` requires `min(8)`** but does not enforce a max attempts cap, dictionary check, or breach-corpus filter. Acceptable for Phase A.\n\n### 5. What was done well\n\n1. **Outbox transaction is single, well-bounded, and correctly sequenced** — `chat.service.ts:53-100` writes user message, assistant message, conversation timestamp, and placeholder inference in one `$transaction`, all before any SDK call.\n2. **Authorization filter table-driven test with coverage guard** — `authorization.filter.ts` + `authorization.filter.test.ts:73-89` will hard-fail the build when a new repository method is added without explicit user-scoping. Excellent regression bait.\n3. **HMAC-over-token instead of raw SHA256** — `session.repository.ts:35-43` requires `SESSION_SECRET` to be set explicitly (no silent fallback), so a DB dump alone cannot forge sessions.\n4. **Cancel/disconnect terminal-state flag** — `stream-orchestrator.ts:46`, `:80`, `:116`, `:141`, `:166` cleanly gate every emit and every state mutation behind a single `terminal` discriminator, which is the right pattern for a re-entrant async orchestrator.\n5. **Builder explicitly documented Open Questions in the LLD and surfaces them in code comments** (e.g., `chat.service.ts:21-24` re: `provider='pending'` sentinel, `session-cookie.ts:3-7` re: cookie name choice). Lowers the cost of cold-reading the code.\n6. **Idempotent seed correctly handles the race window** — `bootstrap/seed.ts:33-37` uses `upsert({ update: {} })` so a concurrent boot can't double-insert and can't corrupt an existing demo user's password.\n\n### 6. Quality score\n\n**7**\n\nSolid Phase A foundation with disciplined TDD and clean separation of concerns. Loses points for the `MessageDto` hydration gap escaping the parallel fix (the controller mapper was never updated), the cancel-path race in the stream orchestrator, the orphaned-on-disconnect `errorCode` not actually persisted anywhere queryable (breaks the frontend's \"interrupted\" UX), the un-correlatable error frames with sentinel `messageId`, and the missing `omittedCount` wire. None of these block merge but all should be fixed before frontend-web integration."}],"stop_reason":"end_turn","stop_sequence":null,"stop_details":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":1,"cache_creation_input_tokens":884,"cache_read_input_tokens":105029,"output_tokens":6877,"server_tool_use":{"web_search_requests":0,"web_fetch_requests":0},"service_tier":"standard","cache_creation":{"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":884},"inference_geo":"","iterations":[{"input_tokens":1,"output_tokens":6877,"cache_read_input_tokens":105029,"cache_creation_input_tokens":884,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":884,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"type":"message"}],"speed":"standard"},"diagnostics":null},"requestId":"req_011CbL5GS36EGAoYb4yCaQsy","attributionAgent":"general-purpose","type":"assistant","uuid":"a3d78f58-cead-463b-b810-b5fbbf4bfb2b","timestamp":"2026-05-23T19:46:43.819Z","userType":"external","entrypoint":"cli","cwd":"/Users/lego/Desktop/personal-projects/argus/.worktrees/phase-a-build","sessionId":"11d45e97-2fff-4114-aafb-b68d865b0473","version":"2.1.150","gitBranch":"HEAD"}
